[37m      [39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mIDENTIFICATION[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mDIVISION[39;49;00m.
[37m      [39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mPROGRAM-ID[39;49;00m.[37m [39;49;00m[31mOCic[39;49;00m.
[37m      *****************************************************************[39;49;00m
[37m      ** This program provides a Textual User Interface (TUI) to the **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** process of compiling and (optionally) executing an OpenCOBOL**[39;49;00m
[37m      ** program.                                                    **[39;49;00m
[37m      **                                                             **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** This programs execution syntax is as follows:               **[39;49;00m
[37m      **                                                             **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** ocic <program-path-and-filename> [ <switch>... ]            **[39;49;00m
[37m      **                                                             **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** Once executed, a display screen will be presented showing   **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** the compilation options that will be used.  The user will   **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** have the opportunity to change options, specify new ones    **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** and specify any program execution arguments to be used if   **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** you select the "Execute" option.  When you press the Enter  **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** key the program will be compiled.                           **[39;49;00m
[37m      **                                                             **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** The SCREEN SECTION contains an image of the screen.         **[39;49;00m
[37m      **                                                             **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** The "010-Parse-Args" section in the PROCEDURE DIVISION has  **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** documentation on switches and their function.               **[39;49;00m
[37m      *****************************************************************[39;49;00m
[37m      **                                                             **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** AUTHOR:       GARY L. CUTLER                                **[39;49;00m
[37m      **               CutlerGL@gmail.com                            **[39;49;00m
[37m      **               Copyright (C) 2009-2010, Gary L. Cutler, GPL  **[39;49;00m
[37m      **                                                             **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** DATE-WRITTEN: June 14, 2009                                 **[39;49;00m
[37m      **                                                             **[39;49;00m
[37m      *****************************************************************[39;49;00m
[37m      ** Note: Depending on which extended DISPLAY handler you're    **[39;49;00m
[37m      **       using (PDCurses, Curses, ...), you may need to un-    **[39;49;00m
[37m      **       comment any source lines tagged with "SCROLL" in cols **[39;49;00m
[37m      **       1-6 in order to have error messages scroll properly   **[39;49;00m
[37m      **       in the OCic shell window.                             **[39;49;00m
[37m      *****************************************************************[39;49;00m
[37m      **  DATE  CHANGE DESCRIPTION                                   **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** ====== ==================================================== **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** GC0609 Don't display compiler messages file if compilation  **[39;49;00m
[37m      **        Is successful.  Also don't display messages if the   **[39;49;00m
[37m      **        output file is busy (just put a message on the       **[39;49;00m
[37m      **        screen, leave the OC screen up & let the user fix    **[39;49;00m
[37m      **        the problem & resubmit.                              **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** GC0709 When 'EXECUTE' is selected, a 'FILE BUSY' error will **[39;49;00m
[37m      **        still cause the (old) executable to be launched.     **[39;49;00m
[37m      **        Also, the 'EXTRA SWITCHES' field is being ignored.   **[39;49;00m
[37m      **        Changed the title bar to lowlighted reverse video &  **[39;49;00m
[37m      **        the message area to highlighted reverse-video.       **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** GC0809 Add a SPACE in from of command-line args when        **[39;49;00m
[37m      **        executing users program.  Add a SPACE after the      **[39;49;00m
[37m      **        -ftraceall switch when building cobc command.        **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** GC0909 Convert to work on Cygwin/Linux as well as MinGW     **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** GC0310 Virtualized the key codes for S-F1 thru S-F7 as they **[39;49;00m
[37m      **        differ depending upon whether PDCurses or NCurses is **[39;49;00m
[37m      **        being used.                                          **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** GC0410 Introduced the cross-reference and source listing    **[39;49;00m
[37m      **        features.  Also fixed a bug in @EXTRA switch proces- **[39;49;00m
[37m      **        sing where garbage will result if more than the      **[39;49;00m
[37m      **        @EXTRA switch is specified.                          **[39;49;00m
[37m      *****************************************************************[39;49;00m

[37m      [39;49;00m[37m   [39;49;00m[34mSCREEN[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mSECTION[39;49;00m.
[37m      *>[39;49;00m
[37m      *> Here is the layout of the OCic screen.[39;49;00m
[37m      *>[39;49;00m
[37m      *> Note that this program can utilize the traditional PC line-drawing characters,[39;49;00m
[37m      *> if they are available.[39;49;00m
[37m      *>[39;49;00m
[37m      *> If this program is run on Windows, it must run with codepage 437 activated to[39;49;00m
[37m      *> display the line-drawing characters.  With a native Windows build or a[39;49;00m
[37m      *> Windows/MinGW build, one could use the command "chcp 437" to set that codepage[39;49;00m
[37m      *> for display within a Windows console window (that should be the default, though).[39;49;00m
[37m      *> With a Windows/Cygwin build, set the environment variable CYGWIN to a value of[39;49;00m
[37m      *> "codepage:oem" (this cannot be done from within the program though - you will[39;49;00m
[37m      *> have to use the "Computer/Advanced System Settings/Environment Variables" (Vista or[39;49;00m
[37m      *> Windows 7) function to define the variable.  XP Users: use "My Computer/Properties/[39;49;00m
[37m      *> Advanced/Environment Variables".[39;49;00m
[37m      *>[39;49;00m
[37m      *> To use OCic without the line-drawing characters, comment-out the first set of[39;49;00m
[37m      *> 78 "LD" items and uncomment the second.[39;49;00m
[37m      *>[39;49;00m
[37m      *> The following sample screen layout shows how the screen looks with line-drawing[39;49;00m
[37m      *> characters disabled.[39;49;00m
[37m      *>[39;49;00m
[37m      *>===================================================================================[39;49;00m
[37m      *> OCic (2010/04/02 11:36) - OpenCOBOL V1.1 Interactive Compilation        Windows 01[39;49;00m
[37m      *> +-----------------------------------------------------------------------------+ 02[39;49;00m
[37m      *> | Program:  OCic                                            F-Key: Select Opt | 03[39;49;00m
[37m      *> | Folder:   E:\OpenCOBOL\Samples                            Enter: Compile    | 04[39;49;00m
[37m      *> | Filename: OCic.cbl                                        Esc:   Quit       | 05[39;49;00m
[37m      *> +-----------------------------------------------------------------------------+ 06[39;49;00m
[37m      *>   On/Off Switches:                                          Configuration:      07[39;49;00m
[37m      *> +---------------------------------------------------------+-------------------+ 08[39;49;00m

[37m      *> | F2   Always make DLLs       F9   Produce xref listing   | S-F2   COBOL85    | 10[39;49;00m
[37m      *> | F3   Pgm is a SUBROUTINE                                | S-F3   COBOL2002  | 11[39;49;00m

[37m      ** specified on the command-line to provide the initial        **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** options shown selected on the screen.  When integrating     **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** OCic into an edirot or framework, include these switches on **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** the ocic.exe command the editor/framework executes.  Any    **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** underlined choice is the default value for that switch.     **[39;49;00m
[37m      **                                                             **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** @CONFIG=BS2000|COBOL85|COBOL2002|DEFAULT|IBM|MF|MVS         **[39;49;00m
[37m      **                                  =======                    **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** This switch specifies the default cobc compiler configura-  **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** tion file to be used                                        **[39;49;00m
[37m      **                                                             **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** @DEBUG=YES|NO                                               **[39;49;00m
[37m      **            ==                                               **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** This switch specifies whether (YES) or not (NO) debugging   **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** lines (those with a "D" in column 7) will be compiled.      **[39;49;00m
[37m      **                                                             **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** @DLL=YES|NO                                                 **[39;49;00m
[37m      **          ==                                                 **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** Use this switch to force ALL compiled programs to be built  **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** as DLLs ("@DLL=YES").  When main programs are built as DLLs **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** they must be executed using the cobcrun utility.  When      **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** "@DLL=NO" is in effect, main programs are generated as      **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** actual "exe" files and only subprograms will be generated   **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** as DLLs.                                                    **[39;49;00m
[37m      **                                                             **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** @EXECUTE=YES|NO                                             **[39;49;00m
[37m      **              ==                                             **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** This switch specifies whether ("@EXECUTE=YES") or not       **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** ("@EXECUTE=NO") the program will be executed after it is    **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** successfully compiled.                                      **[39;49;00m
[37m      **                                                             **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** @EXTRA=extra cobc argument(s)                               **[39;49;00m
[37m      **                                                             **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** This switch allows you to specify additional cobc arguments **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** that aren't managed by the other OC switches.  If used,     **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** this must be the last switch specified on the command line, **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** as everything that follows the "=" will be placed on the    **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** cobc command generated by OC.                               **[39;49;00m
[37m      **                                                             **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** @NOTRUNC=YES|NO                                             **[39;49;00m
[37m      **          ===                                                **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** This switch specifies whether (YES) or not (NO) the sup-    **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** pression of binary field truncation will occur.  If a PIC   **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** 99 COMP field (one byte of storage), for example, is given  **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** the value 123, it may have its value truncated to 23 when   **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** DISPLAYed.  Regardless of the NOTRUNC setting, internally   **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** the full precision of the field (allowing a maximum value   **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** of 255) will be preserved.  Even though truncation - if it  **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** does occur - would appear to have a minimal disruption on   **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** program operation, it has a significant effect on program   **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** run-time speed.                                             **[39;49;00m
[37m      **                                                             **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** @TRACE=YES|NO|ALL                                           **[39;49;00m
[37m      **            ==                                               **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** This switch controls whether or not code will be added to   **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** the object program to produce execution-time logic traces.  **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** A specification of "@TRACE=NO" means no such code will be   **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** produced.  By specifying "@TRACE=YES", code will be genera- **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** ted to display procedure names as they are entered.  A      **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** "@TRACE=ALL" specification will generate not only procedure **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** traces (as "@TRACE=YES" would) but also statement-level     **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** traces too!  All trace output is written to STDERR, so      **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** adding a "2>file" to the execution of the program will pipe **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** the trace output to a file.  You may find it valuable to    **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** add your own DISPLAY statements to the debugging output via **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** "DISPLAY xx UPON SYSERR"  The SYSERR device corresponds to  **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** the Windows or UNIX STDERR device and will therefore honor  **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** any "2>file" placed at the end of your program's execution. **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** Add a "D" in column 7 and you can control the generation or **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** ignoring of these DISPLAY statements via the "@DEBUG"       **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** switch.                                                     **[39;49;00m
[37m      **                                                             **[39;49;00m
[37mGC0410** @SOURCE=YES|NO                                              **[39;49;00m
[37mGC0410**           ==                                                **[39;49;00m
[37mGC0410** Use this switch to produce a source listing of the program, **[39;49;00m
[37mGC0410** PROVIDED it compiles without errors.                        **[39;49;00m
[37m      **                                                             **[39;49;00m
[37mGC0410** @XREF=YES|NO                                                **[39;49;00m
[37mGC0410**           ==                                                **[39;49;00m
[37mGC0410** Use this switch to produce a cross-reference listing of the **[39;49;00m
[37mGC0410** program, PROVIDED it compiles without errors.               **[39;49;00m
[37m      *****************************************************************[39;49;00m

[37m      [39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m011[39;49;00m-[31mInit[39;49;00m.
[37m      [39;49;00m[37m     [39;49;00m[34mMOVE[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m1 [39;49;00m[34mTO[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mI[39;49;00m

[31m                  [39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mINTO[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mSwitch-Keyword-And-Value[39;49;00m

[37m      [39;49;00m[37m         [39;49;00m[34mEND-UNSTRING[39;49;00m
[34m              [39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mIF[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mSwitch-Keyword-And-Value[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[35mNOT [39;49;00m=[37m [39;49;00m[31mSPACES[39;49;00m
[31m                  [39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mUNSTRING[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mSwitch-Keyword-And-Value[39;49;00m
[37m      [39;49;00m[37m                 [39;49;00m[34mDELIMITED[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mBY [39;49;00m[33m'='[39;49;00m
[37m      [39;49;00m[37m                 [39;49;00m[34mINTO[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mSwitch-Keyword[39;49;00m,[37m [39;49;00m[31mSwitch-Value[39;49;00m
[37m      [39;49;00m[37m             [39;49;00m[34mEND-UNSTRING[39;49;00m
[34m                  [39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mPERFORM[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m030[39;49;00m-[31mProcess-Keyword[39;49;00m
[37m      [39;49;00m[37m         [39;49;00m[34mEND-IF[39;49;00m
[34m          [39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mEND-PERFORM[39;49;00m
[34m           [39;49;00m.

[37m      [39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m019[39;49;00m-[31mDone[39;49;00m.
[37m      [39;49;00m[37m     [39;49;00m[34mEXIT[39;49;00m.

[37m      *****************************************************************[39;49;00m
[37m      ** Since this program uses the SCREEN SECTION, it cannot do    **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** conventional console DISPLAY operations.  This routine      **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** (which, I admit, is like using an H-bomb to hunt rabbits)   **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** will submit an "ECHO" command to the system to simulate a   **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** DISPLAY.                                                    **[39;49;00m
[37m      *****************************************************************[39;49;00m
[37m      [39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m021[39;49;00m-[31mBuild-And-Issue-Command[39;49;00m.
[37m      [39;49;00m[37m     [39;49;00m[34mDISPLAY[39;49;00m
[34m              [39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mOutput-Message[39;49;00m
[37m      [39;49;00m[37m     [39;49;00m[34mEND-DISPLAY[39;49;00m
[34m           [39;49;00m.

[37m      [39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m029[39;49;00m-[31mDone[39;49;00m.

[34m                  [39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mWHEN [39;49;00m([31mCS-Char[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([31mI[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m=[37m [39;49;00m[33m'L'[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[35mAND [39;49;00m([31mI[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m<[37m [39;49;00m[34m66[39;49;00m)
[37m      [39;49;00m[37m                 [39;49;00m[34mIF[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mCompressed-Src[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([31mI[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m:[37m [39;49;00m[34m15[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m=[37m [39;49;00m[33m'LINKAGE SECTION'[39;49;00m
[37m      [39;49;00m[37m                     [39;49;00m[34mSET[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m88[39;49;00m-[31mA2-LINKAGE-SECTION[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mTO[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36mTRUE[39;49;00m
[36m                          [39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mGOBACK[39;49;00m
[34m                      [39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mEND-IF[39;49;00m
[34m                  [39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mWHEN [39;49;00m([31mCS-Char[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([31mI[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m=[37m [39;49;00m[33m'I'[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m[35mAND [39;49;00m([31mI[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m<[37m [39;49;00m[34m58[39;49;00m)
[37m      [39;49;00m[37m                 [39;49;00m[34mIF[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mCompressed-Src[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m([31mI[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m:[37m [39;49;00m[34m23[39;49;00m)[37m [39;49;00m=[37m [39;49;00m[33m'IDENTIFICATION '[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m&
[37m      [39;49;00m[37m                                                 [39;49;00m[33m'DIVISION'[39;49;00m
[37m      [39;49;00m[37m                     [39;49;00m[34mSET[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m88[39;49;00m-[31mA2-IDENTIFICATION-DIVISION[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mTO[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[36mTRUE[39;49;00m
[36m                          [39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mGOBACK[39;49;00m

[37m      [39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34m099[39;49;00m-[31mNever-Found-Either-One[39;49;00m.

[37m      [39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mEND[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mPROGRAM[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mCHECKSOURCE[39;49;00m.

[37m      [39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mIDENTIFICATION[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mDIVISION[39;49;00m.
[37m      [39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mPROGRAM-ID[39;49;00m.[37m  [39;49;00m[31mLISTING[39;49;00m.
[37m      *****************************************************************[39;49;00m
[37m      ** This subprogram generates a cross-reference listing of an   **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** OpenCOBOL program.                                          **[39;49;00m
[37m      **                                                             **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** Linkage:      CALL "LISTING" USING <source>                 **[39;49;00m
[37m      **                                    <xref>                   **[39;49;00m
[37m      **                                    <filename>               **[39;49;00m
[37m      **                                                             **[39;49;00m
[37m      **               Where:                                        **[39;49;00m
[37m      **                  <source>   is a PIC X(1) flag indicating   **[39;49;00m
[37m      **                             whether or not a source listing **[39;49;00m
[37m      **                             should be produced (space=NO,   **[39;49;00m
[37m      **                             non-space=yes)                  **[39;49;00m
[37m      **                  <xref>     is a PIC X(1) flag indicating   **[39;49;00m
[37m      **                             whether or not an xref listing  **[39;49;00m
[37m      **                             should be produced (space=NO,   **[39;49;00m
[37m      **                             non-space=yes)                  **[39;49;00m
[37m      **                  <filename> is the [path]filename of the    **[39;49;00m
[37m      **                             program being listed and/or     **[39;49;00m
[37m      **                             xreffed in a PIC X(256) form.   **[39;49;00m
[37m      *****************************************************************[39;49;00m
[37m      **                                                             **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** AUTHOR:       GARY L. CUTLER                                **[39;49;00m
[37m      **               CutlerGL@gmail.com                            **[39;49;00m
[37m      **               Copyright (C) 2010, Gary L. Cutler, GPL       **[39;49;00m
[37m      **                                                             **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** DATE-WRITTEN: April 1, 2010                                 **[39;49;00m
[37m      **                                                             **[39;49;00m
[37m      *****************************************************************[39;49;00m
[37m      **  DATE  CHANGE DESCRIPTION                                   **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** ====== ==================================================== **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** GC0410 Initial coding                                       **[39;49;00m
[37m      ** GC0710 Handle duplicate data names (i.e. "CORRESPONDING" or **[39;49;00m
[37m      **        qualified items) better; ignore "END PROGRAM" recs   **[39;49;00m
[37m      **        so program name doesn't appear in listing.           **[39;49;00m
[37m      *****************************************************************[39;49;00m

[37m      [39;49;00m[37m     [39;49;00m[34mSELECT[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mReport-File[39;49;00m[37m          [39;49;00m[34mASSIGN[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[34mTO[39;49;00m[37m [39;49;00m[31mReport-Filename[39;49;00m
